<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="lesson-3-measurement-of-disease-occurrence-vital-statistics">Lesson 3: MEASUREMENT OF DISEASE OCCURRENCE (VITAL STATISTICS)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#lesson-3-measurement-of-disease-occurrence-vital-statistics" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="objectives">Objectives<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#objectives" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>At the end of the lesson the learner will be able to: -</p>
<ol>
<li>Discuss the measurements of disease occurrence</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="1-0-introduction">1.0. INTRODUCTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#1-0-introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Measurement is fundamental to Epidemiologic practice</li>
<li>Epidemiological studies are designed to Identify disease determinants, describe and compare disease trends and evaluate public health interventions aimed at controlling health problems</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="2-0-measures-of-disease-frequency">2.0. MEASURES OF DISEASE FREQUENCY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-0-measures-of-disease-frequency" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Measures of disease frequency in mathematical terms – count, proportion (percentage), rate and ratio</li>
<li>Measures of disease frequency in epidemiology - prevalence and incidence</li>
<li>Importance of Denominator</li>
</ul>
<p>a → Numerator
b → Denominator</p>
<ul>
<li>Example</li>
<li>500 cases of malaria in Turkana and 120 cases of malaria in Moshi</li>
<li>Which one is more infected? Turkana: 200/800,000 = 0.25/1,000 (25%) and Moshi: 120/300,000 = 0.4/1,000 (40%)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="counts">Counts<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#counts" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Number of cases</li>
<li>On its own offers little information</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="ratio">Ratio<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#ratio" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>The division of two numbers (unrelated)</li>
<li>Numerator not included in the denominator</li>
<li>Allows comparison of quantities of different nature</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="proportion">Proportion<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#proportion" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>The division of 2 numbers (related)</li>
<li>Numerator always included in the denominator</li>
<li>Quantities have to be of same nature</li>
<li>Proportion always ranges between 0 and 1</li>
<li>Percentage = proportion × 100</li>
</ul>
<p>Carey Francis Okinda © 2015</p>
<p>Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="rate">Rate<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#rate" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The division of 2 numbers
Time included in the denominator</p>
<ul>
<li>Speed of occurrence of an event over time</li>
<li>Rate may be expressed in any power of 10: - 100, 1000, 10000, 100 000...</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="3-0-sources-of-morbidity-and-mortality-data">3.0. SOURCES OF MORBIDITY AND MORTALITY DATA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#3-0-sources-of-morbidity-and-mortality-data" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p><strong>RECALL:</strong>
What are the causes of morbidity and mortality?</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="4-0-measurement-of-morbidity-disease-occurrence">4.0. MEASUREMENT OF MORBIDITY (DISEASE OCCURRENCE)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-0-measurement-of-morbidity-disease-occurrence" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Is the measurement of the amount of disease in a given population?</li>
<li>It is measured in terms of incidence and prevalence rates.</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251226-1513f773.jpeg" alt="img-8.jpeg">
Diagram 3.1: Relationship between Incidence and Prevalence</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="4-1-incidence">4.1. INCIDENCE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-1-incidence" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Incidence = number of new cases of a disease occurring in a specified time period divided by the number of individuals at risk of developing the disease during the same time</li>
<li>Incidence of a disease is defined as the number of new cases of a disease that occur during a specified period of time in a population at risk for developing the disease</li>
</ul>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Incidence</mtext><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;New&nbsp;cases&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;specified&nbsp;period</mtext><mtext>Population&nbsp;at&nbsp;risk&nbsp;during&nbsp;the&nbsp;period</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Incidence} = \frac{\text{Number of New cases in a specified period}}{\text{Population at risk during the period}} \times 1000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Incidence</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.2519em; vertical-align: -0.8804em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3714em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Population&nbsp;at&nbsp;risk&nbsp;during&nbsp;the&nbsp;period</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;New&nbsp;cases&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;specified&nbsp;period</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8804em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1000</span></span></span></span></span></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-2-prevalence">4.2. PREVALENCE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-2-prevalence" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Prevalence = <strong>total</strong> number of affected individuals in a population at a specified time period divided by the number of individuals in the population at the time</li>
<li>This is the proportion of a defined group having a disease at a given point in time</li>
<li>It is the number of affected persons present in the population at a specific time divided by the number of persons in the population at that time</li>
<li>Chronic diseases have high prevalence rates</li>
<li>Low prevalence rate of a disease indicates that the disease is fatal or gets cured easily</li>
</ul>
<p>Prevalence = <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mfrac><mtext>No&nbsp;of&nbsp;cases&nbsp;of&nbsp;a&nbsp;disease&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;population&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;specified&nbsp;period</mtext><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;persons&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;population&nbsp;at&nbsp;that&nbsp;specified&nbsp;time</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\frac{\text{No of cases of a disease in the population in a specified period}}{\text{Number of persons in the population at that specified time}} \times 1000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.4133em; vertical-align: -0.4811em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.9322em;"><span style="top: -2.655em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;persons&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;population&nbsp;at&nbsp;that&nbsp;specified&nbsp;time</span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.4461em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">No&nbsp;of&nbsp;cases&nbsp;of&nbsp;a&nbsp;disease&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;population&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;specified&nbsp;period</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.4811em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1000</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-3-risk-of-a-disease">4.3. RISK OF A DISEASE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-3-risk-of-a-disease" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Risk is the probability that an individual with some characteristics (e.g. age, race, gender, etc.) will experience a health status change over a specified follow-up time (risk period)</li>
<li>Estimated by observing events among a population during a specified time</li>
<li>Measures of risk in epidemiology include absolute risk, relative risk and attributable risk</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="absolute-risk">Absolute Risk<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#absolute-risk" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>This is the incidence or prevalence of a disease in a population</li>
<li>Indicates the magnitude of the risk in a group of people with a certain disease</li>
</ul>
<p>Ratio of risk (or of the incidence rate) = <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mfrac><mtext>Disease&nbsp;risk&nbsp;in&nbsp;exposed</mtext><mtext>Disease&nbsp;risk&nbsp;in&nbsp;non-exposed</mtext></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\frac{\text{Disease risk in exposed}}{\text{Disease risk in non-exposed}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.4133em; vertical-align: -0.4811em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.9322em;"><span style="top: -2.655em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Disease&nbsp;risk&nbsp;in&nbsp;non-exposed</span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.4461em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Disease&nbsp;risk&nbsp;in&nbsp;exposed</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.4811em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Difference in risks (incidence rate) = Disease risk (exposed) – Disease risk (non-exposed)</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="relative-risk-rr-or-odds-risk-or">Relative Risk (RR) or Odds Risk (OR)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#relative-risk-rr-or-odds-risk-or" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>RR is the ratio of incidence of disease in exposed individuals to the incidence of disease in non-exposed individuals (from a cohort/prospective study)</li>
</ul>
<p>Relative Risk (RR) = <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mfrac><mtext>Risk&nbsp;in&nbsp;exposed</mtext><mtext>Risk&nbsp;in&nbsp;non-exposed</mtext></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\frac{\text{Risk in exposed}}{\text{Risk in non-exposed}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.4133em; vertical-align: -0.4811em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.9322em;"><span style="top: -2.655em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Risk&nbsp;in&nbsp;non-exposed</span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.4461em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Risk&nbsp;in&nbsp;exposed</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.4811em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Incidence in exposed = <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a/(a + b)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Incidence in non-exposed = <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>c</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c/(c + d)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>RR = <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mfrac><mtext>Incidence&nbsp;in&nbsp;exposed</mtext><mtext>Incidence&nbsp;in&nbsp;non-exposed</mtext></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mi>c</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>c</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\frac{\text{Incidence in exposed}}{ \text{Incidence in non-exposed} } = \frac{a/(a + b)}{c/(c + d)}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.4133em; vertical-align: -0.4811em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.9322em;"><span style="top: -2.655em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Incidence&nbsp;in&nbsp;non-exposed</span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.4461em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Incidence&nbsp;in&nbsp;exposed</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.4811em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.53em; vertical-align: -0.52em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.01em;"><span style="top: -2.655em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span><span class="mord mtight">/</span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.485em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">a</span><span class="mord mtight">/</span><span class="mopen mtight">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">a</span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">b</span><span class="mclose mtight">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.52em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul>
<li>Interpretation</li>
<li>RR = 1 - Risk in exposed equal risk in non-exposed (No association)</li>
<li>RR &gt; 1 - Risk in exposed greater than risk in non-exposed (positive association, possibly causal)</li>
<li>RR &lt; 1 - Risk in exposed less than risk in non-exposed (Negative association, possibly protective)</li>
</ul>
<table><thead><tr><th></th><th>True Diagnosis</th><th></th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Test Results</td><td>Disease</td><td>No Disease</td><td>Total</td></tr><tr><td>Positive</td><td>a (TP) 132</td><td>b (FP) 985</td><td>a + b (TP + FP) 1117</td></tr><tr><td>Negative</td><td>c (FN) 47</td><td>d (TN) 62, 295</td><td>c + d (FN + TN) 62, 342</td></tr><tr><td>Total</td><td>a + c (TP + FN)</td><td>b + d (FP+TN)</td><td>a + b + c + d (TP + FP + FN + TN)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>RR = Incidence in exposed = a/(a + b)
Incidence in non-exposed = c/(c + d)</p>
<p>RR = 132/1117
47/62, 342</p>
<p>= 0.118
0.00075</p>
<p>= 157 (Risk in exposed &gt; risk in non-exposed)</p>
<ul>
<li>OR is the ratio of the odds that cases were exposed to the odds that controls were exposed (from a case control/retrospective study), is an estimate of the RR</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="attributable-risk-ar-attributable-fraction-af">Attributable Risk (AR)/Attributable Fraction (AF)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#attributable-risk-ar-attributable-fraction-af" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>AR is the amount of disease incidence that can be attributed to a specific exposure</li>
<li>AF is the proportion of disease incidence that can be attributed to a specific exposure (among those who were exposed)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="5-0-measurement-of-mortality">5.0. MEASUREMENT OF MORTALITY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#5-0-measurement-of-mortality" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>This is the measure of the amount death in a community</li>
<li>Mortality rates include crude death rate (CDR), case specific death rate (CSDR), crude fatality rate (CFR), infant mortality rate (IMR) and maternal mortality rate (MMR)</li>
</ul>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="crude-death-rate-cdr">Crude Death Rate (CDR)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#crude-death-rate-cdr" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>CDR is the total number of deaths to residents in a specified geographic area (country, state, county, etc.) divided by the total population for the same geographic area (for a Specified time period, usually a calendar year) and multiplied by 1000</li>
</ul>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi><mi>R</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mtext>No.&nbsp;of&nbsp;deaths&nbsp;within&nbsp;a&nbsp;year</mtext><mtext>Total&nbsp;mid-year&nbsp;population</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">CDR = \frac{\text{No. of deaths within a year}}{\text{Total mid-year population}} \times 1,000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.2519em; vertical-align: -0.8804em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3714em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Total&nbsp;mid-year&nbsp;population</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">No.&nbsp;of&nbsp;deaths&nbsp;within&nbsp;a&nbsp;year</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8804em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8389em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">000</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="case-specific-death-rate-csdr">Case Specific Death rate (CSDR)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#case-specific-death-rate-csdr" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Measures the number of deaths attributed to a specific cause in a year divided by the total population that year</li>
</ul>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Cause&nbsp;specific&nbsp;death&nbsp;rate</mtext><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;death&nbsp;due&nbsp;to&nbsp;a&nbsp;particular&nbsp;cause&nbsp;(defined&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</mtext><mtext>Mid-period&nbsp;population&nbsp;(same&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Cause specific death rate} = \frac{\text{Number of death due to a particular cause (defined place and time period)}}{\text{Mid-period population (same place and time period)}} \times 1,000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Cause&nbsp;specific&nbsp;death&nbsp;rate</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.363em; vertical-align: -0.936em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.427em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Mid-period&nbsp;population&nbsp;(same&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;death&nbsp;due&nbsp;to&nbsp;a&nbsp;particular&nbsp;cause&nbsp;(defined&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.936em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8389em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">000</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="crude-fatality-rate-cfr">Crude Fatality rate (CFR)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#crude-fatality-rate-cfr" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Measures the proportion of episodes of illness that result in death</li>
<li>Number of people who die from a disease out of those who had the disease within a given period of time divided by the number of cases of that disease in a given period</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="infant-mortality-rate-imr">Infant Mortality rate (IMR)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#infant-mortality-rate-imr" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Number of children who die before they are less than one year old per 1000 live births</li>
</ul>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-error" title="ParseError: KaTeX parse error: Expected 'EOF', got '&amp;' at position 71: …ath to infants &amp;̲lt;1 year of ag…" style="color: rgb(204, 0, 0);">\text{Infant mortality rate} = \frac{\text{Number of death to infants &amp;lt;1 year of age (defined place and time period)}}{\text{Number of live births (same place and time period)}} \times 1,000</span></div>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Infant&nbsp;mortality&nbsp;rate&nbsp;in&nbsp;Laos&nbsp;in&nbsp;2005</mtext><mo>∼</mo><mn>70</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Infant mortality rate in Laos in 2005} \sim 70 / 1,000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Infant&nbsp;mortality&nbsp;rate&nbsp;in&nbsp;Laos&nbsp;in&nbsp;2005</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∼</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">70/1</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">000</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Age-specific&nbsp;death&nbsp;rate</mtext><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;death&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;particular&nbsp;age&nbsp;group&nbsp;(defined&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</mtext><mtext>Mid-period&nbsp;population&nbsp;(same&nbsp;age&nbsp;group,&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Age-specific death rate} = \frac{\text{Number of death in a particular age group (defined place and time period)}}{\text{Mid-period population (same age group, place and time period)}} \times 1,000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; <div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="maternal-mortality-rate-mmr">Maternal Mortality rate (MMR)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#maternal-mortality-rate-mmr" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Number of women who die as a result of child bearing in a given year per 1000 live births</li>
</ul>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>MMR</mtext><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;maternal&nbsp;deaths&nbsp;due&nbsp;to&nbsp;child&nbsp;bearing</mtext><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;live&nbsp;births&nbsp;per&nbsp;year</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{MMR} = \frac{\text{Number of maternal deaths due to child bearing}}{\text{Number of live births per year}} \times 1000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">MMR</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.2519em; vertical-align: -0.8804em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3714em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;live&nbsp;births&nbsp;per&nbsp;year</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;maternal&nbsp;deaths&nbsp;due&nbsp;to&nbsp;child&nbsp;bearing</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8804em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1000</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<ul>
<li>Mortality rate: Death of a particular disease/event in the total population (e.g., maternal mortality)</li>
</ul>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mfrac><mrow><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;pregnancy</mtext><mo>−</mo><mtext>related&nbsp;death&nbsp;(defined&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</mtext></mrow><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;live&nbsp;birth&nbsp;(same&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>100</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\frac{\text{Number of pregnancy} - \text{related death (defined place and time period)}}{\text{Number of live birth (same place and time period)}} \times 100,000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.363em; vertical-align: -0.936em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.427em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;live&nbsp;birth&nbsp;(same&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;pregnancy</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">related&nbsp;death&nbsp;(defined&nbsp;place&nbsp;and&nbsp;time&nbsp;period)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.936em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8389em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">100</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">000</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>Maternal mortality rate in Laos in 2000 ~ 530/100,000</p>

<ul>
<li>The major direct causes of maternal morbidity and mortality include haemorrhage, infection, high blood pressure (eclampsia), unsafe abortion, prolonged and obstructed labour and other indirect causes including HIV/AIDS, malaria and TB, heart disease, anaemia</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="factors-contributing-to-maternal-mortality">Factors Contributing To Maternal Mortality<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#factors-contributing-to-maternal-mortality" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Difficulty of predicting and/or preventing obstetric complications</li>
<li>Lack of access to good quality maternal health services</li>
<li>Poor health before and during pregnancy</li>
<li>Women's low social and economic status</li>
<li>Biological factors e.g. age, parity</li>
</ol>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251226-e9c2cd64.jpeg" alt="img-11.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="6-0-measurement-of-fertility">6.0. MEASUREMENT OF FERTILITY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#6-0-measurement-of-fertility" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="crude-birth-rate-cbr">Crude Birth rate (CBR)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#crude-birth-rate-cbr" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Number of live births in a year divided by the total population in a year</li>
</ul>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>CBR</mtext><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;live&nbsp;births&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;year</mtext><mtext>Total&nbsp;population&nbsp;that&nbsp;year</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{CBR} = \frac{\text{Number of live births in a year}}{\text{Total population that year}} \times 1000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">CBR</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.2519em; vertical-align: -0.8804em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3714em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Total&nbsp;population&nbsp;that&nbsp;year</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;live&nbsp;births&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;year</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8804em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1000</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="general-fertility-rate-gfr">General Fertility rate (GFR)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#general-fertility-rate-gfr" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Measure of fertility</li>
</ul>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mtext>GFR</mtext><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;live&nbsp;births&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;year</mtext><mtext>Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;women&nbsp;of&nbsp;child&nbsp;bearing&nbsp;age&nbsp;that&nbsp;year</mtext></mfrac><mo>×</mo><mn>1000</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{GFR} = \frac{\text{Number of live births in a year}}{\text{Number of women of child bearing age that year}} \times 1000</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">GFR</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.2519em; vertical-align: -0.8804em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3714em;"><span style="top: -2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;women&nbsp;of&nbsp;child&nbsp;bearing&nbsp;age&nbsp;that&nbsp;year</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top: -3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Number&nbsp;of&nbsp;live&nbsp;births&nbsp;in&nbsp;a&nbsp;year</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8804em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1000</span></span></span></span></span></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="lesson-4-descriptive-epidemiology">Lesson 4: DESCRIPTIVE EPIDEMIOLOGY<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#lesson-4-descriptive-epidemiology" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="objectives">Objectives<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#objectives" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>At the end of the lesson the learner will be able to: -</p>
<ol>
<li>Explain disease occurrence using the person-place-time model</li>
<li>Explain how 'person' variables determine disease occurrence</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="1-0-introduction">1.0. INTRODUCTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#1-0-introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Descriptive epidemiology is the study of the amount and distribution of disease or health status within a population by person, place and time</li>
<li>Involves determination of incidence, prevalence and mortality rates for diseases in large population groups according to characteristics such as age, sex, race (person) and geographical areas (place) as well as time distribution (cases per day, month, year)</li>
<li>The <strong>person-place-time</strong> model describes disease occurrence in terms of <strong>who</strong> is affected by the disease (person), <strong>where</strong> the cases are (place) and <strong>when</strong> the disease occurs (time)</li>
<li>These variables interact in a way that favours or does not favour the development of disease in an individual (the three variables must interact)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="2-0-the-person">2.0. THE PERSON<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-0-the-person" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Personal characteristics influence one's exposure and susceptibility to disease. These characteristics include: -</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>Age</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Single most important determinant of disease</li>
<li>Diseases can be classified based on age e.g. childhood diseases; diseases of the elderly</li>
<li>Diseases differ in terms of severity and frequency according to one's age</li>
<li>Age determines occupation</li>
<li>Can be used as the basis for determining type of risk factors</li>
</ul>
<ol start="2">
<li>Sex</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Influences disease occurrence</li>
<li>Rate of death is higher for males than females in all age groups (why?)</li>
<li>Some diseases affect specific sex e.g. cancer of the cervix (females) and cancer of the prostate (males)</li>
<li>Determines risk factors</li>
</ul>
<ol start="3">
<li>Occupation</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Contributes to different rates of morbidity and mortality</li>
<li>Determine type and amount of risk factors</li>
</ul>
<p>Carey Francis Okinda © 2015
This document is available on
studocu
Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<ol start="4">
<li>Marital status and family</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>High marriage rate is a good indicator of prosperity</li>
<li>Mortality rates are lower in married people</li>
<li>Some diseases are influence by marital status – e.g. breast cancer is low in married women than unmarried because breast feeding is protective against breast cancer</li>
</ul>
<ol start="5">
<li>
<p>Education
Discuss how this affects disease occurrence</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Social class</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Ethnicity(race)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Racial differences interact with other factors to determine the occurrence and frequency of diseases</li>
<li>Skin colour may influence occurrence of rickets since black skin pigmentation absorbs more sunlight which promotes natural synthesis of vitamin D</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="3-0-place">3.0. PLACE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#3-0-place" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Is the basis for describing the distribution of population and diseases</li>
<li>Frequency of disease occurrence can be related to the place of occurrence as specified by natural barriers such as mountains, rivers, deserts or political/administrative boundaries because they influence environmental conditions e.g. iodine deficiency is common in highland and swampy places where soil is deficient of iodine; fluorosis is common where water has an excessively high content of fluorine</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-0-time">4.0. TIME<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-0-time" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Disease occurrence is dependent on what time of the month or year e.g. nutrient deficiency diseases become common after a period of drought</li>
<li>Occurrence of some disease can be predicted as they conform to cyclic disease trends e.g. malnutrition, colds, malaria</li>
<li>Some cannot be predicted that is they conform to secular trends e.g. Ebola</li>
<li>Time trends</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251226-1a7e8436.jpeg" alt="img-12.jpeg"></p>
<p>Carey Francis Okinda © 2015
Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="lesson-5-epidemiological-study-designs">Lesson 5: EPIDEMIOLOGICAL STUDY DESIGNS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#lesson-5-epidemiological-study-designs" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="objectives">Objectives<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#objectives" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>At the end of the lesson the learner will be able to: -</p>
<ol>
<li>Describe different types of epidemiological studies/designs</li>
<li>State advantages and disadvantages of each study design</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="1-0-introduction">1.0. INTRODUCTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#1-0-introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Epidemiological information is collected by conducting a study in the community</li>
<li>It is difficult to collect information from all members of the community hence the need to sample the population</li>
<li>Qualitative designs</li>
<li>Are complementary to quantitative designs, are important in study of social determinants of health problems</li>
<li>Qualitative methods include focus group discussion (FGDs), interviews, surveys, self-reports, observations and document analysis</li>
<li>Sampling is mainly purposive and quality assurance is attained through trustworthiness (credibility, conformability, dependability, transferability) and authenticity(fairness, ontological, educative, tactical, catalytic)</li>
<li>Quantitative designs</li>
<li>Goal is to understand the frequency and causes of health-related phenomena</li>
<li>Seek causes by describing associations between exposures (causes) and outcomes</li>
<li>Quantitative methods include observational, experimental and mixed</li>
<li>Sampling is random (simple, stratified, cluster, etc.) or purposive</li>
<li>Quality assurance is through reliability and validity</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="2-0-choosing-a-design">2.0. CHOOSING A DESIGN<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-0-choosing-a-design" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Purpose of the study
a. Hypothesis-testing versus hypothesis generating
b. Finding signal versus quantifying the signal</li>
<li>Available resources</li>
<li>Need for data collection</li>
<li>Choice of outcome</li>
<li>Ability to draw valid causal inference</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="3-0-epidemiological-study-designs">3.0. EPIDEMIOLOGICAL STUDY DESIGNS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#3-0-epidemiological-study-designs" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Broadly grouped as experimental and non-experimental (observational).</li>
<li>Observational studies are further sub classified as descriptive and analytical</li>
<li>Analytical designs can be case-controlled or cohort while descriptive can be cross-sectional, correlational and case series</li>
</ul>
<p>Carey Francis Okinda © 2015
This document is available on
studocu
Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<ul>
<li>Experimental studies can be clinical or community trials (randomized or non-randomized)</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251226-c4834d7f.jpeg" alt="img-13.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-0-observational-non-experimental-designs">4.0. OBSERVATIONAL (NON-EXPERIMENTAL) DESIGNS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-0-observational-non-experimental-designs" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-1-descriptive-studies">4.1. DESCRIPTIVE STUDIES<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-1-descriptive-studies" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Provide information on patterns of disease occurrence</li>
<li>Descriptive statistics generated can be correlated with clinical observations or laboratory studies to generate hypotheses</li>
<li>Often provide clues about disease causation that can be pursued by more sophisticated research designs</li>
<li>Three critical dimensions for describing a health condition are – person, place &amp; time</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="advantages">Advantages<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#advantages" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ol>
<li>Uses routinely collected, readily available data</li>
<li>Less expensive and time-consuming</li>
<li>Good for assessing prevalence and patterns of disease occurrence</li>
<li>Useful in the formulation of research hypotheses – suggestive of risk factors</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="disadvantages">Disadvantages<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disadvantages" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ol>
<li>Usually cannot test epidemiologic hypotheses</li>
<li>Lacks comparison group</li>
</ol>
<p>Carey Francis Okinda © 2015</p>
<p>Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<ol start="3">
<li>Cannot usually discern a temporal relationship between an exposure and disease</li>
<li>Not useful for rare events</li>
<li>May be subject to selection bias due to refusal, death, etc.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="types">Types<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#types" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Main types of descriptive studies include correlational studies, case reports and case series and cross-sectional studies</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-1-1-correlational-studies">4.1.1. CORRELATIONAL STUDIES<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-1-1-correlational-studies" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Measure of association: correlation coefficient (r)</li>
<li>Linear association between exposure and outcome, ranging from -1 to 1</li>
<li>Examples</li>
<li>Correlation of rate of a given disease and average amount of caloric intake, proportion of smokers, or median income</li>
<li>Death rates from coronary artery disease correlate with per capita cigarette sales</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="uses-of-correlational-studies">Uses of Correlational Studies<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#uses-of-correlational-studies" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>To suggest disease causation</li>
<li>To describe broad social and cultural attributes affecting health</li>
<li>Surveillance</li>
<li>To evaluate disease control measures Correlational Studies Summary</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="advantages">Advantages<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#advantages" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Quick and relatively inexpensive</li>
<li>May be able to use readily available data</li>
<li>Useful in hypothesis generation</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="disadvantages">Disadvantages<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disadvantages" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Does not provide information about the relationship between risk factor levels and disease in individuals</li>
<li>Ecologic fallacy – association observed between variables on an aggregate level does not necessarily represent the association at an individual level</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-1-2-case-reports-and-case-series">4.1.2. CASE REPORTS AND CASE SERIES<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-1-2-case-reports-and-case-series" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Case reports and case series are observational, descriptive research designs.</li>
<li>A case report is an in depth discussion of a patient's diagnosis, the intervention(s) used, and the outcome(s) achieved</li>
<li>Case reports are typically conducted on one or two patients.</li>
<li>A case series is a descriptive analysis of a series of patients with common characteristic(s) such as having a similar diagnosis or receiving a similar intervention</li>
</ul>
<p>Carey Francis Okinda © 2015
This document is available on
33
studocu
Downloaded by Patrick Ngobiro (<a href="mailto:pngobiro@gmail.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">pngobiro@gmail.com</a>)</p>
<ul>
